name:G‍u‍e‍s‍t‍ ‍U‍s‍e‍r
info:Superior Suite
info:Stayed in May 2024
info:Couples
info:5 Reviews
rating:4.8
posted:Posted May 21, 2024
msg:As an old five-star hotel in Wuxi, Degen Hotel is indeed in an excellent location and has very good service. I booked 2 superior suites for 2 nights. Because there is only one suite on each floor, the two suites are located on different floors and have different layouts. The entire facility is a bit old, but it is sufficient. It is located in the Chong'an Temple business district, surrounded by shopping malls such as Hang Lung and Great Eastern. You can go out to find food at 10 o'clock at night. It takes only 2 minutes to walk downstairs to Sanyang Plaza. The transportation is extremely convenient. If you travel by car, guests staying in the hotel can park for free in the Huaguang Building parking lot. There is an affordable beverage cabinet on the first floor, which can be purchased by face recognition... The service is also very good. I bought McDonald's on the first night, but accidentally knocked it over in the elevator waiting area on the first floor. I told the front desk with guilt, and someone handled it immediately. They also told the surrounding guests to be careful. In the middle of the night on the first night, my daughter grabbed the quilt, so I called the room service at 5 am to add a quilt, and they responded quickly. Finally, I lost a piece of jade when I checked out. Jade is not worth much, but because it was given by my parents when I was young, it is of great commemorative value to me. I contacted the hotel the next day and helped find it. I arranged for the courier to send it back as soon as possible. Thank you very much... Having said so many good places, there are of course places that can be improved. First, the door handle of Suite 3423 where I stayed was blocked and needed to be turned with force. Second, compared with most star-rated hotels, the buffet breakfast has room for improvement in terms of the variety and taste of the dishes... Overall, the flaws do not cover the merits. As an old star-rated hotel, Degen Hotel is indeed a good choice for Wuxi tourism accommodation

I would stumble when I stepped out of it. Handrails should be added on the outside.
Environment: From the lobby to the room, it always feels dark for some reason. This is the first time I have felt this way when staying in a hotel. There is a protruding half wall in the room. I will hit it when I go to the window. The quilt has no edges at all.

Seeing as it was a hotel, I added breakfast. There are few varieties and they are unpalatable, so there is no supplement. I fed myself with porridge and water, and finally ordered takeout.

The door lock was stuck this morning, so I asked my aunt to help. Tell me there is a small arm to press it, I said the red and black one, it is stuck and cannot be pressed. Then I repeatedly asked her to look for the little arm. I thought it was a mechanism and touched the door all over. Finally, I asked her to take a photo to see what kind of arm it was. Then wrap it in a towel and press the buckle hard, and finally open it. When my aunt came back, she said inexplicably and repeatedly that it must be because you didn't close the door properly and couldn't open it😅
During breakfast, two waiters were in the dining room and had a loud argument over the placement of things.
The overall feeling is not good, 300-400 is acceptable, 700 is not worth it, and it cannot compete with chain hotels.

My feet are already frozen. Let's go back to the room quickly. By the way, the room temperature in this hotel is not high. It is set to 35 degrees, but the actual temperature is always around 20 degrees. I waited for 40 minutes, but no one answered me. I called the front desk again this time. A girl answered the phone. She told me that the master had checked it and said that the gym had not been used for a long time. The central air conditioner needs time to heat up, which caused the situation just now. I told her that this is not right. No matter how cold the air conditioning pipe is, I turned it on when I came to the hotel. It is still cold after 40 or 50 minutes. I am afraid it is not a problem that the system needs to be preheated? Then, the girl suggested that I go down and take a look. The temperature should be almost up. Since they have checked it and repaired it, I still have doubts in my heart. Facing the desire to lift iron, I embarked on a freezing journey for the second time. This time when I walked into the gym, the fire came up all of a sudden. Not only did it not heat up, but it was even colder than before, freezing cold! I communicated with the front desk again in the ice-cold environment of the gym. I said to the girl, can you take charge of this matter so far? It’s better to call the manager to talk to me because it’s too cold here! I booked your hotel because it has a gym. I won’t exercise today and I want a refund. The answer given by the front desk girl this time was to find the leader and asked me to go back to the room and wait for news. I will call back in 10 minutes. I went back to the room and the phone rang soon. First, the refund was not allowed, but the room type could be upgraded. Second, two heaters had been moved in, and I was asked to exercise in half an hour. I looked at the watch and it was ten o'clock. Half an hour later, it would be half past ten. I was asked to lift weights at half past ten in the evening? I was furious. I said, I don’t like to exercise at midnight, and I now suspect that it will still be cold there half an hour later. 
This matter has made me furious so far. I came to this hotel for exercise. Can you make up for my time loss by giving me a presidential suite? I want a corn to fill my stomach, and you said you would open the way for your Porsche. I would like to ask the supervisor Degen, do I need it? An arrogant attitude that you must be good if you are given a little discount, is this the way your hotel treats guests? I tell you, I don’t need your superior room, my planned fitness has gone down the drain, I need to apologize and compensate. Unfortunately, until I left the hotel, no one in this Degen Hotel said sorry, haha.
As a traveler who travels for business all year round, facing such a tough and domineering hotel, I am helpless. Fitness is impossible. It’s almost eleven o’clock, and the temperature has dropped to freezing point, so I gave up the idea of ​​changing hotels. I feel extremely humiliated and angry. To be honest, this is the first time. No matter how bad the hotel in Harbin is, it will not treat guests as dogs without bones. And this Degen has done it, perfect! Degen Hotel, in your hearts, you are all the fathers of the guests, right? **That’s it, the air conditioner blows cold air in the winter, right? There is no way, we are like this. You want to refund the money, right? There is no way, it’s impossible. You can change places to live, or upgrade, you can choose or not, if you don’t choose, get out! Kneel down to Degen Hotel!
Here, brothers and sisters who want to come, avoid the pit. I use my humiliating experience to give you advice. I strongly do not recommend choosing this hotel. If you want to feel how the hotel is a guest's father, welcome to stay! 
Finally, I suggest that you look at the reviews to choose a hotel. This time, for fitness, I didn't look at the reviews, and I was careless! Most of the negative reviews of this hotel are very objective, the breakfast is extremely poor, the service attitude is arrogant, the decoration is old, and the air conditioner does not heat. The key is that if you want to experience being abused, insulted, and treated as a father, please skip the above.

msg:這已經是我們第二次入住德根。作為老牌的酒店，服務是真的一流，剛進酒店大堂就有專人幫着一起拉行李，還會幫忙送到電梯口，問打掃衞生的阿姨要小朋友的拖鞋也特別熱情，給了我們兩雙。有地下停車場，方便停車。出了酒店走兩分鐘就是三陽地鐵站，交通非常便利。周圍商場林立，不管買什麼都很方便，外賣也很豐富。美中不足的就是外賣不能送上樓，需要自己下去拿。對小朋友不太友好的是衞生間的設計，特別浴缸那裡，玻璃無法移動，給小朋友洗澡的時候還要探半個身子進去才能開花灑，這就非常的不方便，出門在外，還是比較喜歡淋浴的衞生間。電視機也比較老，沒辦法投屏。不過總體來説德根飯店還是不錯的，國慶期間沒有瘋狂漲價，性價比還是挺高的。下次去無錫的話還是會考慮入住。

msg:地理位置處於無錫市中心商業區，吃喝玩樂不愁、100 m開外就是地鐵站、訂車速達！有免費停車場。
門僮迎客開關車門、禮貌問候；前臺中規中矩、大堂整潔整齊！
房間色彩搭配柔和、布草潔凈、大玻璃窗陽光灑滿全房、大沙發供客曬太陽休憇俱佳、帶小冰箱……！
早餐完全可以滿足普通消費需求！環境也整潔舒適！
服務（客房、餐廳）體現出酒店有針對性的要求、培訓、管理！
………！
有別於與價格不相上下的商務酒店、精品酒店與三星四星酒店，有服務意識與行動，這個在酒店業中逐漸缺失，望保持！
個人後續來錫將再度選擇德根飯店入住！
幾點建議：
避免餐廳的管理人員身着便服、徒手整理餐枱、食物擺放台！
餐廳的小雲吞湯料，胡椒粉可以讓顧客視個人口味喜好添加，因為也有少數人不喜歡辣味！
大堂的泰國餐廳似乎與酒店的服務不一致，也許是外包？對住店客人不太熱情！聊天什麼的是常態！與酒店整體不協調！

msg:五星級酒店，名不副實
首先，房間燈光昏暗，所有燈都打開仍然覺得暗
其次，衞生不合格，馬桶圈上甚至有尿漬，難以想象這種情況實在五星級的酒店碰到的
第三，沒有淋浴房，淋浴衹能在浴缸裏，很不方便。淋蓬頭還漏水
第四，早飯種類很少，而且兩天的菜色是一模一樣的，炒麪還是冷的
最後，服務意識也跟不上。早餐餐廳門口都沒有前台，我進去的時候還早，餐廳裏沒有人，我差點以為走錯地方。過了會兒，我在拿菜了，服務生才出來問我房號
總之，這個酒店無論是衞生還是設施亦或是服務沒有一點擔得起他的星級。
唯一的優點大概就是地理位置優越，旁邊就是商業圈，離地鐵站也很近。除此之外，一無是處

rating:3.7
posted:Posted June 13, 2021
msg:環境挺好，衞生可以，市中心老酒店，停車在隔壁地下，能理解。
恆隆就在路對面，很方便。
不足地方：隔音極差，門四周一圈都透光的，電梯聲，別的房間關門聲，大清早過道放的音樂，一覽無餘……
浴缸等設施，跟其他五星還是有點小差距。
空調非常非常差勁，風門打鐵的聲音明顯，空調運行聲音很大，製冷效果很差，門外過道比房間涼快，設定24度自動風，1分鐘吹風，1分鐘停止運行，衹能改固定中等風狀態，而且製冷效果很差。

msg:Mites are everywhere in every corner. I checked in at 10.10 in the morning. After washing, I put on the quilt and found that my skin was a little itchy. I didn't want to move, so I ignored it. At noon, I also had some mite allergies - urticaria. I called the hotel at 12 noon to check the reason for the room. Then check out. At 4 o'clock in the afternoon, erythema began to appear on a large area of ​​​​the skin. When I called the hotel, the staff expressed their ignorance and added WeChat. They did not admit that there was any unclean place during the communication. It has been 10 days since we came out and we have been staying in hotels. We have not had such allergic reactions, and allergic reactions are rapid. After the communication was fruitless, we called 110 and 12345 and went to the hotel front desk for processing. The manager never came forward and the hotel staff did not admit any responsibility. After the police's persuasion, the hotel compensated us with 212 yuan for the cost of the pharmacy. We were also disheartened. The city of Wuxi should not be like this! On the evening of the 11th, my condition began to worsen, and I contacted the manager. His attitude was very tough, and the communication was fruitless. Around 10pm on the evening of the 11th, I went to the Dermatology Depar**ent of the First Affiliated Hospital of Suzhou University and it was confirmed that it was measles caused by allergies. After applying the medicine on the 12th, my skin improved. I communicated with the hotel again on the 12th and still did not admit any fault. The review is just for those who have high standards of hygiene to be cautious before entering!
